*air¹
/eə(r) ||; ɛr/noun
1 [U] the mixture of gases that surrounds the earth and that people, animals and plants breathe 空气: the pure mountain air 山中清纯的空气 Open a window -- I need some fresh air. 把窗户打开，我需要呼吸点新鲜空气。 The air was polluted by smoke from the factory. 空气被工厂喷出来的烟雾污染了。
2 [U] the space around and above things 空中；天空: to throw a ball high into the air 把球抛到空中 in the open air (= outside) 在户外
3 [U] travel or transport in an aircraft 航空；空运: to travel by air 乘飞机旅行 an air ticket 飞机票
4 [sing] an air (of sth) the particular feeling or impression that is given by sb/sth 神态；气质；气氛: She has a confident air. 她一副满怀信心的样子。
a breath of fresh air→BREATH clear the air→CLEAR³ in the air probably going to happen soon 酝酿中: A feeling of change was in the air. 人们可以感觉到将要实行变改。 in the open air→OPEN¹ on (the) air sending out programmes on the radio or television 广播中: This radio station is on the air 24 hours a day. 这家电台每天24小时全日广播。 vanish, etc into thin air→THIN¹
air²
/eə(r) ||; ɛr/verb
1 [I,T] to put clothes, etc in a warm place or outside in the fresh air to make sure they are completely dry; to become dry in this way 晾，风干（衣服等）: Put the sheets on the washing line to air. 把床单挂在晾衣绳上晾干。
2 [I,T] to make a room, etc fresh by letting air into it; to become fresh in this way 使通风；透气 · Open the window to air the room. 打开窗户让房间通通风。
3 [T] to tell people what you think about sth 提出、发表意见: The discussion gave people a chance to air their views. 这次讨论给了大家一个发表意见的机会。

airtime
/ˈeətaɪm ||; ˈɛrˌtaɪm/noun [U]:
1 the amount of time that is given to a subject on radio or television （电台或电视节目就某主题的）广播时间
2 the amount of time that is paid for when you use aMOBILE PHONE(= a telephone that you can carry around with you) （使用移动电话要付费的）通话时间: This deal gives you 90 minutes free airtime a week. 这交易每星期给你90分钟免费通话时间。

ˌair-to-ˈair
adj (usually before a noun 通常用于名词前) from one aircraft to another while they are both flying 空对空的（从一空中飞机对另一空中飞机）: an air-to-air missile 空空导弹

ˌair ˌtraffic conˈtroller
noun [C] a person whose job is to organize routes for aircraft, and to tell pilots by radio when they can land and take off 空中交通管制人员

airwaves
/ˈeəweɪvz ||; ˈɛrˌwevz/noun [pl] radio waves that are used in sending out radio and television programmes （用于播送电台和电视节目的）无线电波: A well-known voice came over the airwaves. 电波传来一个熟悉的声音。

airway
/ˈeəweɪ ||; ˈɛrˌwe/noun [C] (medical医学) the passage from your nose and throat down into your lungs, through which you breathe （鼻子和喉部通往肺部的）气道

airworthy
/ˈeəwɜ:ði ||; ˈɛrˌwɝðɪ/adj (used about aircraft 指飞机) safe to fly 适航的 ➔airworthiness noun [U]

/ˈeəri ||; ˈɛrɪ/adj having a lot of fresh air inside 有充足新鲜空气的；通风的

/aɪl ||; aɪl/noun [C] a passage between the rows of seats in a church, theatre, etc （教堂、戏院等中两排座位之间的）通道

*alarm¹
/əˈlɑ:m ||; əˈlɑrm/noun
1 [U] a sudden feeling of fear or worry 惊慌；不安: She jumped up in alarm. 她惊慌地跳了起来。
2 [sing] a warning of danger 警报: A small boy saw the smoke and raised the alarm. 一个小男孩见到冒烟马上呼救。
3 [C] a machine that warns you of danger, for example by ringing a loud bell 警报器: The burglars set off the alarmwhen they broke the window. 盗贼破窗而入的时候触响了警报器。 The fire / burglar alarmwent off in the middle of the night. 半夜里，火警警铃／防盗警铃响了。
4 [C] =ALARM CLOCK
a false alarm→FALSE
alarm²
/əˈlɑ:m ||; əˈlɑrm/verb [T] to make sb/sth feel suddenly frightened or worried 使惊慌；惊动

(also alarm) noun [C] a clock that you can set to make a noise at a particular time to wake you up 闹钟: She set the alarm clock for half past six. 她把闹钟设定在六点半。 ☞picture at clock 见 clock 插图

albatross
/ˈælbətrɒs ||; ˈælbəˌtrɔs/noun[C]
1 a very large white seabird with long wings that lives in the Pacific and Southern Oceans 信天翁（一种白色大海鸟，翼长，生活在太平洋及南方海洋） ☞picture at seabird 见 seabird 插图
2 [usu.sing] (written 书面语) a thing that causes problems or that prevents you from doing sth 苦恼；障碍: The national debt is an albatross around the President's neck. 国债是总统的一大包袱。

*alcohol

/əˈlaɪt ||; əˈlaɪt/adj on fire; burning 着火；燃烧着: A cigarette set the petrol alight. 香烟点燃了汽油。 Alight can only be used after a noun, but you can use burning before a noun The whole building was alight. a burning building. alight 只能用于名词后，名词前可以用 burning：The whole building was alight. 整幢建筑物都着火了。a burning building 燃烧着的建筑物。

*alive
/əˈlaɪv ||; əˈlaɪv/adj
1 not dead; living 活着；有生命: The young woman was still alive when the ambulance reached the hospital. 救护车到达医院时，那个年轻女人还活着。 The quick action of the doctors kept the child alive. 医生及时行动，保全了孩子的性命。
Alive can only be used after a noun, but you can use living before a noun Are her parents still alive? Does she have any living relatives? alive 只能用于名词后，名词前可以用 living：Are her parents still alive? 她父母亲仍然健在吗？ Does she have any living relatives? 她还有亲戚在世吗？
2 continuing to exist 继续存在；尚存: Many old traditions are very much alive in this area of the country. 在该国的这一地区，许多旧传统依然保留着。
3 full of life 充满生机；富有生气: In the evening the town really comes alive. 到了晚上，城里就真的变得生气勃勃。

alkali
/ˈælkəlaɪ ||; ˈælkəˌlaɪ/noun [C,U] a chemical substance that can burn skin when it is dissolved in water. An alkali has a pH value of more than 7. 碱 ☞Look at acid and base. 参看 acid 及 base。 ☞picture at pH 见 pH 插图 ➔alkaline adj

alkaloid
/ˈælkəlɔɪd ||; ˈælkəˌlɔɪd/noun [C] a poisonous substance that is found in some plants. Some alkaloids are used in drugs. 生物碱（有毒，见于某些植物中，有的可用作药物）

alkane
/ˈælkeɪn ||; ˈælken/noun [C] any of a series of gases that contain HYDROGEN and CARBON 链烷，烷烃（含氢和碳的气体）: Methane and propane are alkanes. 甲烷和丙烷是链烷。

alkene
/ˈælki:n ||; ˈælkin/noun [C] any of a series of gases that contain HYDROGEN and CARBON and that have a doubleBOND(= force of attraction)holding atoms together 链烯，烯烃（含氢和碳的气体，由双键将原子连在一起）

*all¹
/ɔ:l ||; ɔl/det pronoun
1 the whole of a thing or of a period of time 全部；所有: All (of) the food has gone. 食物全部吃光了。 They've eaten all of it. 他们把它都吃光了。 They've eaten it all. 他们把它都吃光了。 This money is all yours. 这笔钱全是你的。 All of it is yours. 这都是你的。 all week/month/year 整个星期；整个月；全年 He worked hard all his life. 他一生都辛勤工作。
2 every one of a group 全体；所有: All (of) my children can swim. 我的孩子都会游泳。 My children can all swim. 我的孩子都会游泳。 She's read all (of) these books. 这些书她全看过。 She's read them all. 这些她全看过。 The people at the meeting all voted against the plan. 所有与会者都投票反对那个计划。 All of them voted against the plan. 他们都投票反对那个计划。
3 everything that; the only thing that 一切；唯一: I wrote down all I could remember. 我能记得的都写了下来。 All I've eaten today is one banana. 我今天只吃了一个香蕉。
above all→ABOVE after all→AFTER for all
1 in spite of 虽然；尽管: For all her wealth and beauty, she was never very happy. 尽管她又有钱又漂亮，但她根本不快活。
2 used to show that sth is not important or of no interest or value to you （用于表示对某事不重视或不感兴趣）: For all I know, he's probably remarried by now. 就我所知，他现在很可能又结婚了。
in all in total 总共；合计: There were ten of us in all. 我们一共十人。 not all that... not very 并不十分…: The film wasn't all that good. 那部电影并不十分好。 (not) at all (not) in any way 一点也（不）；根本（不）: I didn't enjoy it at all. 我一点也不喜欢它。 We can say not at all as a reply when somebody thanks us for something. 有人向我们致谢时，我们可以说 not at all 答礼。
 *all²
/ɔ:l ||; ɔl/adv
1 completely; very 完全；非常: He has lived all alone since his wife died. 他妻子去世后，他一直独居。 I didn't watch that programme -- I forgot all about it. 我没有看那个节目。我完全忘了这回事。 They got all excited about it. 他们对此都十分兴奋。
2 (in sport) for each side （体育）各方: The score was two all. 双方都得两分。
all along from the beginning 从一开始；一直: I knew you were joking all along. 我从一开始就知道你在开玩笑。 all the better, harder, etc even better, harder, etc than before 比以前好；比以前更难等: It will be all the more difficult with two people missing. 两个人失踪，事情更难办了。

all-
/ɔ:l ||; ɔl/prefix (used in adjectives and adverbs 用于构成形容词及副词)
1 completely 全部；完全: an all-American show 全由美国人演出的表演 an all-inclusive price 包括一切的价格
2 in the highest degree 最高程度: all-important 首要的 all-powerful 有无上权力的

allergic
/əˈlɜ:dʒɪk ||; əˈlɝdʒɪk/adj

2 caused by an allergy 由过敏引起的: an allergic reaction to house dust 对屋内灰尘的过敏反应

allergy

ˈall out
adj adv using all your strength, etc 竭尽全力: an all-out effort 全力以赴

*allow
/əˈlaʊ ||; əˈlaυ/verb[T]
1 allow sb/sth to do sth;allow sth to give permission for sb/sth to do sth or for sth to happen 允许: Children under eighteen are not allowed to buy alcohol. 十八岁以下的孩子不准购买酒精饮料。 I'm afraid we don't allow people to bring dogs into this restaurant. 对不起，带狗不能进本餐厅。 Photography is not allowed inside the cathedral. 大教堂内不准拍照。
Compare allow, permit and let. Allow can be used in both formal and informal English. The passive form be allowed to is especially common. Permit is a formal word and is usually used only in written English. Let is an informal word, and very common in spoken English. You allow sb to do sth but let sb do sth (no ‘to’). Let cannot be used in the passive Visitors are not allowed/permitted to smoke in this area. Smoking is not allowed/permitted. I'm not allowed to smoke in my bedroom. My dad won't let me smoke in my bedroom. 比较 allow、permit 及 let。allow 可以用于正式或非正式场合。被动式 be allowed to 尤其常用。permit 用于正式场合，通常只作书面语。let 用于非正式场合，常用于口语。我们说 allow sb to do sth，但 let sb do sth（不用to）。let 不用于被动语态：Visitors are not allowed／permitted to smoke in this area. 访客不得在这个范围内抽烟。Smoking is not allowed／permitted. 不准吸烟。I'm not allowed to smoke in my bedroom. 我在卧房内不可以抽烟。My Dad won't let me smoke in my bedroom. 我爸爸不让我在卧房内抽烟。
2 to give permission for sb/sth to be or go somewhere 准许（在或前往某处）: No dogs allowed. 不得携犬入内。 I'm only allowed out on Friday and Saturday nights. 我只有星期五、星期六晚上才可以出去。
3 allow sb sth to let sb have sth 赋予；给与；允许: My contract allows me four weeks' holiday a year. 根据合约，我每年有四个星期假期。
4 allow sb/sth to do sth to make it possible for sb/sth to do sth 使…可以做某事: Working part-time would allow me to spend more time with my family. 非全日工作使我有多点时间跟家人相聚。
5 allow sth (for sb/sth) to provide money, time, etc for sb/sth 提供，拨出（金钱、时间等）: You should allow about 30 minutes for each question. 每道试题你大约要给30分钟做。
allow for sb/sth to think about possible problems when you are planning sth and include extra time, money, etc for them 顾及；考虑到；把…计算在内: The journey should take about two hours, allowing for heavy traffic. 把交通繁忙的因素计算在内的话，整个旅程需时两个小时左右。

ˌall ˈright
(informal 非正式alright) exclamation adv adj (not before a noun 不用于名词前)
1 good enough; OK 还好；还可以: Is everything all right? 一切顺利吗？
2 safe; not hurt; well 安全；没受伤；健康: I hope the children are all right. 我希望孩子们都很好。 Do you feel all right? 你还好吧？
3 showing you agree to do what sb has asked; OK （用于表示同意）: ‘Can you get me some stamps?’ ‘Yes, all right.’ “你能给我买些邮票来吗？”“好的，没问题。”
You say ‘That's all right,’ when sb thanks you for sth or when sb says sorry for sth he/she has done ‘Thanks for the lift home.’ ‘That's (quite) all right.’ ‘I'm so sorry I'm late.’ ‘That's all right. We haven't started yet anyway.’ 当某人表示感谢或表示歉意时，你可以说 That's all right： 'Thanks for the lift home.' 'That's (quite) all right.'“谢谢你让我搭你的车回家。”“没有什么。”'I'm so sorry I'm late.' 'That's all right. We haven't started yet anyway.'“对不起，我迟到了。”“没关系。反正我们还没有开始呢。”

*almost
/ˈɔ:lməʊst ||; ˈɔlˌmost/adv very nearly; not quite 几乎；差不多；差一点: By nine o'clock almost everybody had arrived. 到了九时，差不多所有人都到达了。 Careful! *alone
/əˈləʊn ||; əˈlon/adj adv
1 without any other person 单独；独自: The old man lives alone. 那个老人独自居住。 Are you alone? Can I speak to you for a moment? 你单独一个人吗？我跟你谈一会儿，行吗？ I don't like walking home alone after dark. 天黑以后，我不喜欢一个人走回家。
Alone and lonely both mean that you are not with other people. Lonely (US lonesome) means that you are unhappy about this, but alone does not usually suggest either happiness or unhappiness. Alone cannot be used before a noun. You can also use on your own and by yourself to mean ‘alone’. These expressions are more informal and very common in spoken English. alone 和 lonely 都指单独一人。lonely（美 lonesome）表示对这种情况感到不快乐；alone 则不表示快乐与否。alone 不可以用于名词之前。也可以用 on your own 和 by yourself 来表达“alone”的意思。这些词语多用于非正式的场合，常用于口语。
2 (after a noun or pronoun 用于名词或代词后) only 只有；仅: You alone can help us. 只有你才能帮我们。 The rent alone takes up most of my salary. 单单房租就花去我的大部份薪金。
go it alone to start working on your own without the usual help 独自干 leave sb/sth alone→LEAVE¹ let alone→LET

*along
/əˈlɒŋ; US əˈlɔ:ŋ ||; əˈlɔŋ/prep adv
1 from one end to or towards the other end of sth 从一端到另一端: I walked slowly along the road. 我沿着那条路慢慢地走。 David looked along the corridor to see if anyone was coming. 戴维向走廊的另一端望去，看看有没有人走过来。
2 on or beside sth long 在长形物上；在长形物旁边；沿着: Wild flowers grew along both sides of the river. 河两岸长着野花。 Our house is about halfway along the street. 我家大约在街的中段。
3 forward 向前: We moved along slowly with the crowd. 我们随着人群慢慢往前移动。
4 (informal 非正式) with sb 一起: We're going for a walk. Why don't you come along too? 我们去散步。一块儿去好吗？
all along→ALL² along with sb/sth together with sb/sth 与…在一起 go along with sb/sth to agree with sb's ideas or plans 赞同（某人的主意或计划）

*already
/ɔ:lˈredi ||; ɔlˈrɛdɪ/adv
1 used for talking about sth that has happened before now or before a particular time in the past （用于说话前或过去某时间已发生的事）已经: ‘Would you like some lunch?’ ‘No, I've already eaten, thanks.’ “你吃不吃午餐？”“不，我吃过了，谢谢。” We got there at 6.30 but Marsha had already left. 我们六点半到达那儿，但是马莎已经走了。 Sita was already awake when I went into her room. 我走进西塔房间时，她已经醒了。
2 (used in negative sentences and questions for expressing surprise) so early; as soon as this （用于否定句及疑问句，表示惊奇）这么早，这么快: Have you finished already? 你已经做完啦？ Surely you're not going already! 你不是现在就去吧！

*also
/ˈɔ:lsəʊ ||; ˈɔlso/adv (not with negative verbs 不与否定动词连用) in addition; too 也；亦；而且: He plays several instruments and also writes music. 他会奏几种乐器，还会作曲。 Bring summer clothing and also something warm to wear in the evenings. 带上夏天的衣服，还要带上几件晚上穿的暖和的衣服。 The food is wonderful, and also very cheap. 食物好吃，而且价钱低廉。 Too and as well are less formal than also and are very common in spoken English. Also usually goes before a main verb or after ‘is’, ‘are’, ‘were’, etc He also enjoys reading. He has also been to Australia. He is also intelligent. Too and as well usually go at the end of a phrase or sentence I really love this song, and I liked the first one too/as well. too 和 as well 常用于口语，而 also 则适用于较正式的场合。 also 常用于主要动词之前，或用于 is、are、were 等之后：He also enjoys reading. 他也喜欢阅读。He has also been to Australia. 他也去过澳大利亚。He is also intelligent. 他也很聪明。too 和 as well 通常在短语末或句末：I really love this song, and I liked the first one too/as well. 我很喜欢这首歌，也很喜欢第一首。 not only ... but also→ONLY

alternate¹
/ɔ:lˈtɜ:nət; US ˈɔ:ltərnət ||; ˈɔltɚnət/adj
1 (used about two types of events, things, etc) happening or following regularly one after the other （指两种事物）轮流的: There will be alternate periods of sun and showers tomorrow. 明天时晴时雨。
2 one of every two 每两个中的一个的；间隔的: He works alternate weeks (= he works the first week, he doesn't work the second week, he works again the third week, etc). 他隔周工作。 ➔alternately adv The bricks were painted alternately white and red. 砖块交替漆成白色和红色。
alternate²
/ˈɔ:ltəneɪt ||; ˈɔltɚˌnet/verb
1 [I] alternate with sth;alternate between A and B (used about two types of events, things, etc) to happen or follow regularly one after the other （指两种事物）轮流发生: Busy periods in the hospital alternate with times when there is not much to do. 医院工作时忙时闲。 She seemed to alternate between hating him and loving him. 她似乎时而恨他，时而爱他。
2 [T] alternate A with B to cause two types of events or things to happen or follow regularly one after the other 使交替；使轮流发生: He alternated periods of work with periods of rest. 他让生活劳逸相间。 ➔alternation /ˌɔ:ltəˈneɪʃn ||; ˌɔltɚˈneʃən/ noun [C,U]

alˌternate ˈangles
noun [pl] (mathematics数学) two angles, formed on opposite sides of a line that crosses two other lines. If the two lines that are crossed are PARALLEL (= always the same distance apart), the alternate angles are equal. 错角 ☞picture at angle 见 angle 插图

ˌalternating ˈcurrent
noun [C,U] (abbr AC) a flow of electricity that changes direction regularly many times a second 交流电 ☞Compare direct current. 与 direct current 比较。

alternative¹
/ɔ:lˈtɜ:nətɪv ||; ɔlˈtɝnətɪv/adj (only before a noun 只用于名词前)
1 that you can use, do, etc instead of sth else 取代的；替代的: The motorway was closed so we had to find an alternative route. 高速公路关闭了，我们不得不改走别的道路。
2 different to what is usual or traditional 不同于平常的或传统的: alternative medicine 非传统药物 ➔alternatively adv
alternative²
/ɔ:lˈtɜ:nətɪv ||; ɔlˈtɝnətɪv/noun [C] an alternative (to sth) one of two or more things that you can choose between 可供选择的事物: What can I eat as an alternative to meat? 不吃肉，我别的能吃什么？ There are several alternatives open to us at the moment. 现在我们有好几个选择。

alternator
/ˈɔ:ltəneɪtə(r) ||; ˈɔltɚˌnetɚ/noun [C] a device, used especially in a car, that produces electrical current that moves in different directions 交流发电机（尤用于汽车）

*although
/ɔ:lˈðəʊ ||; ɔlˈðo/ conj
1 in spite of the fact that 虽然；尽管: Although she was tired, she stayed up late watching television. 她虽然很累，但仍然看电视，很晚还不睡觉。
2 and yet; but 然而；但是: I love dogs, although I wouldn't have one as a pet. 我很喜欢狗，但我不愿意把狗当作宠物来饲养。
Though and although are the same but at the end of a sentence it is only possible to use though She knew all her friends would be at the party. She didn't want to go, though. Even though can be used for emphasis She didn't want to go, although/though/even though she knew all her friends would be there. though 和 although 的意思相同，但句末只能用though：She knew all her friends would be at the party. She didn't want to go, though. 她知道她所有的朋友都会出席那个聚会，但是她不想去。even though 用于加强语气：She didn't want to go, although／though／even though she knew all her friends would be there. 虽然她知道她所有的朋友都会出席，但是她不想去。
altimeter
/ˈæltɪmi:tə(r) ||; ˈæltəˌmitɚ/noun [C] an instrument for showing height above sea level, used especially in an aircraft 高度计（尤用于飞机）

altitude
/ˈæltɪtju:d; US -tʌ:d ||; ˈæltəˌtud/noun
1 [sing] the height of sth above sea level 海拔: The plane climbed to an altitude of 10000 metres. 那架飞机爬升到海拔10000米。
2 [C] [usu.pl] a place that is high above sea level 海拔甚高之处；高处；高地: You need to carry oxygen when you are climbing at high altitudes. 攀登高处时，需要带备氧气。

alto
/ˈæltəʊ ||; ˈælto/noun [C] (plural altos) the lowest normal singing voice for a woman, the highest for a man; a woman or man with this voice 女低音（歌手）；男声最高音（歌手）

*altogether
/ˌɔ:ltəˈgeðə(r) ||; ˌɔltəˈgɛðɚ/adv
1 completely 完全；全面: I don't altogether agree with you. 我不完全同意你的意见。 At the age of 55 he stopped working altogether. 到了55岁，他完全停止工作。 This time the situation is altogether different. 这一回的情况完全不同。
2 including everything; in total 总计；全部: How much money will I need altogether? 我总共需要多少钱？ Altogether there were six of us. 我们总共六人。
3 when you consider everything; generally 总的看来；一般而言: Altogether, this town is a pleasant place to live. 总的来说，这个镇是一个舒适的居住地方。
Altogether is not the same as all together. All together means ‘everything or everybody together’ Put your books all together on the table. Let's sing. All together now! altogether 和 all together 不相同。all together 表示“全部一起”的意思：Put your books all together on the table. 将你的书全部放在桌子上。Let's sing. All together now! 我们唱吧。大家一起唱！

*always
/ˈɔ:lweɪz ||; ˈɔlwez/adv
1 at all times; regularly 总是；经常: I always get up at 6.30. 我总是六点半起床。 Why is the train always late when I'm in a hurry? 为什么我每一次赶时间列车都误点？
2 all through the past until now 一向；素来: Tony has always been shy. 托尼向来害羞。 I've always liked music. 我一向喜爱音乐。
3 for ever 永远: I shall always remember this moment. 这一刻将令我毕生难忘。
4 (only used with continuous tenses 只与进行时连用) again and again, usually in an annoying way 一再（通常指令人讨厌地）: She's always complaining about something. 她总是抱怨这个抱怨那个。
5 used with ‘can’ or ‘could’ for suggesting sth that sb could do, especially if nothing else is possible （与 can 或 could 连用，表示可以做某事，尤其是在没有其他办法的时候）: If you haven't got enough money, I could always lend you some. 如果你钱不够，我总是可以借给你一些。
Always does not usually go at the beginning of a sentence. It usually goes before the main verb or after ‘is’, ‘are’, ‘were’, etc He always wears those shoes. I have always wanted to visit Egypt. Fiona is always late. However, always can go at the beginning of a sentence when you are telling somebody to do something Always stop and look before you cross the road. always 通常不用于句子的开头，而用于主要动词之前，或用于 is、are、were 等之后：He always wears those shoes. 他总是穿这双鞋。I have always wanted to visit Egypt. 我一直希望到埃及去看看。Fiona is always late.菲奥纳总是迟到。如要某人做某事，always 可以放在句首：Always stop and look before you cross the road. 每次过马路都要先停步，看清楚。

*ancient

*and
/ənd;ən;strong form ænd ||; ənd; ən; ænd/ conj
1 (used to connect words or parts of sentences) also; in addition to （用于连接词语或句子的组成部份）和，还有，而且: a boy and a girl 一个男孩和一个女孩 Do it slowly and carefully. 慢慢来，小心地做。 We were singing and dancing all evening. 我们整晚都在唱歌跳舞。 Come in and sit down. 进来坐下吧。
When the two things are closely linked, you do not need to repeat the ‘a’, etc a knife and fork my father and mother 如果两种事物密切相关，就不须要重复a等冠词：a knife and fork 刀叉 my father and mother 我父母亲
2 (used when you are saying numbers in sums) in addition to; plus （用于算术）加: Twelve and six is eighteen. 十二加六等于十八。
When you are saying large numbers and is used after the word ‘hundred ’ We say 2264 as two thousand, two hundred and sixty-four. 如果要说大数目，hundred 之后用 and：We say 2264 as two thousand, two hundred and sixty-four. 2264用英语表达就说 two thousand, two hundred and sixty-four。
3 used between repeated words to show that sth is increasing or continuing （用于重复的词中间）越来越…；重复地: The situation is getting worse and worse. 情况越来越坏。 I shouted and shouted but nobody answered. 我喊了又喊，但是没有人应我。
4 used instead of ‘to’ after certain verbs, for example ‘go’, ‘come’, ‘try’ 用于某些动词如 go、come、try 等之后，代替 to: Go and answer the door for me, will you? 你帮我去应门好吗？ Why don't you come and stay with us one weekend? 为何不来我们这里度一个周末？ I'll try and find out what's going on. 我会设法查明到底是怎么回事。

*angle¹
/ˈæŋgl ||; ˈæŋgḷ/noun[C]

*another
/əˈnʌðə(r) ||; əˈnʌðɚ/det pronoun
1 one more person or thing of the same kind 又一个，再一个（同类的人或物）: Would you like another drink? 你要再来一杯吗？ They've got three children already and they're having another. 他们已经生了三个孩子，而现在又要再生一个了。
2 a different thing or person 不同的一个；另一: I'm afraid I can't see you tomorrow. Could we arrange another day? 我明天恐怕不能见你了，我们另约一天见面好吗？ If you've already seen that film, we can go and see another. 如果你已经看过那部电影，我们可以去看另一部。
one after another/the other→ONE¹ yet another→YET

*answer¹
/ˈɑ:nsə(r); US ˈænsər ||; ˈænsɚ/verb[I,T]
1 to say or write sth back to sb who has asked you sth or written to you 回答；答复: I asked her what the matter was but she didn't answer. 我问她发生了什么事，但她没有回答。 I've asked you a question, now please answer me. 我已经问了你一个问题，现在请你回答。 Answer all the questions on the form. 回答表格上的所有问题。 He hasn't answered my letter yet (= written a letter back to me). 他还没有给我回信。 When I asked him how much he earned, he answered that it was none of my business. 我问他赚了多少钱，他回答说这不关我的事。 ‘No!’ he answered angrily. “不！”他生气地答道。
Answer and reply are the most common verbs used for speaking or writing in reaction to questions, letters, etc I asked him a question but he didn't answer. I sent my application but they haven't replied yet. Note that you answer a person, a question or a letter (no ‘ to ’) but you reply to a letter. Respond is less common and more formal with this meaning Applicants must respond within seven days. It is more commonly used with the meaning of ‘reacting in a way that is desired’ Despite all the doctor's efforts the patient did not respond to treatment. 回答问题、覆信等最常用的动词是 answer 和 reply：I asked him a question but he didn't answer. 我问了他一个问题，但他没有回答。I sent my application but they haven't replied yet. 我寄了申请信，但他们还没有回复。答复别人问题或回信可以说 answer a person, a question or a letter（不加 to），但是回信也可以说 reply to a letter。respond（意指“答复”）较少用，但适用于较正式的场合：Applicants must respond within seven days. 申请人须于七天内回复。Respond 通常指“有预期反应”﹕Despite all the doctor's efforts the patient did not respond to treatment. 虽然医生用了各种方法，但病人身体对治疗没有反应。
2 to do sth as a reply 以行动回复: Can you answer the phone (= pick up the receiver) for me, please? 请替我接听电话好吗？ I rang their doorbell but nobody answered. 我按了他们的门铃，但是没有人应门。
answer back to defend yourself against sth bad that has been written or said about you 答辩；辩护 answer (sb) back to reply rudely to sb 回嘴；顶嘴；顶撞 answer for sb/sth
1 to accept responsibility for sth/sb 对某人或某事负责；为…承担起责任: Somebody will have to answer for all the damage that has been caused. 总得有人对所造成的一切损毁负责。
2 to speak in support of sb/sth 发言支持
*answer²
/ˈɑ:nsə(r); US ˈænsər ||; ˈænsɚ/noun [C] an answer (to sb/sth)
1 something that you say, write or do as a reply 答复；回复；作为回复的行动: The answer to your question is that I don't know. 对于你的问题，我的答复是：不知道。 They've made me an offer and I have to give them an answerby Friday. 他们向我提了建议，我最迟星期五得回复。 I wrote to them two weeks ago and I'm still waiting for an answer. 我两个星期前写信给他们，到现在还没有回音。 I knocked on the door and waited but there was no answer. 我敲了敲门，等了一会儿却没有人应门。
2 a solution to a problem 解决办法: I didn't have any money so the only answer was to borrow some. 我没有钱，只好向人家借一些。
3 a reply to a question in a test or exam 答案: My answer to question 5 was wrong. 我第5题答错了。 How many answers did you get right? 你答对了几道题？
4 the correct reply to a question in a test or exam 正确答案: What was the answer to question 4? 第4道题的正确答案是什么？
in answer (to sth) as a reply (to sth) 作为（对某事的）答复

answerable
/ˈɑ:nsərəbl ||; ˈænsɚəbḷ/ answerable to sb (for sth) having to explain and give good reasons for your actions to sb; responsible to sb 向某人负责

/ˈɑ:nsəfəʊn ||; ˈænsɚˌfon/ (brit also 英亦作 answerphone) noun [C] a machine that answers the telephone and records messages from the people who call 电话录音机: I rang him and left a message on his answering machine. 我给他打了电话，并在他的电话录音机上留了个口信。

/ˌæntɪˈsi:dnt ||; ˌæntəˈsidṇt/noun[C]

2 antecedents [pl] the people in sb's family who lived a long time ago 祖先 [SYN] ancestors 同义词为 ancestors
3 (grammar语法) a word or phrase to which the following word, especially a pronoun, refers 先行词；先行语: In ‘He grabbed the ball and threw it in the air’, ‘ball’ is the antecedent of ‘it’. 在 He grabbed the ball and threw it in the air 这一句中，ball 是 it 的先行词。

*anxious
/ˈæŋkʃəs ||; ˈæŋkʃəs/adj
1 anxious (about/for sb/sth) worried and afraid 担忧的；忧虑的；焦虑不安的: I'm anxious about my exam. 我为考试担忧。 I began to get anxious when they still hadn't arrived at 9 o'clock. 他们9点钟还没有到达，我开始担忧起来。 an anxious look/expression 担忧的样子／表情
2 causing worry and fear 令人担忧的: For a few anxious moments we thought we'd missed the train. 我们以为错过了列车，担心了一会儿。
3 anxious to do sth;anxious for sth wanting sth very much 渴望 ➔anxiously adv

*any
/ˈeni ||; ˈɛnɪ/det pronoun adv
1 (used instead of some in negative sentences and in questions 用于否定句及疑问句，取代some) We didn't have any lunch. 我们没有吃午餐。 I speak hardly any (= almost no) Spanish. 我完全不会说西班牙语。 Do you have any questions? 你有什么问题吗？ I don't like any of his books. 他的书我都不喜欢。
Look at the note at some. 参看 some 的注释。
2 used for saying that it does not matter which thing or person you choose （用于表示任何或随便）: Take any book you want. 你想拿哪本书就拿好了。 Come round any time -- I'm usually in. 什么时候来都可以，我通常都在。 I'll take any that you don't want. 你不要的我都要。
3 (used in negative sentences and questions 用于否定句及疑问句) at all; to any degree 完全；任何程度: I can't run any faster. 我没有办法跑得更快。 Is your father any better? 你父亲好一点没有？
any moment/second/minute/day (now) very soon 很快: She should be home any minute now. 她很快就会到家。

*anybody
/ˈenibɒdi ||; ˈɛnɪˌbɑdɪ/ (also anyone) pronoun
1 (usually in questions or negative statements 通常用于疑问句或否定陈述句) any person 任何人: I didn't know anybody at the party. 聚会上的人，我一个也不认识。 Is there anybody here who can speak Japanese? 这里有人会说日语吗？ Would anybody else (= any other person) like to come with me? 还有人想跟我来吗？
The difference between somebody and anybody is the same as the difference between some and any. Look at the notes at some and somebody. somebody 和 anybody 之间的差别与 some 和 any 的差别一样。参看 some 及 somebody 的注释。
2 any person, it does not matter who 任何人（不管是谁）；谁都: Anybody (= all people) can learn to swim. 人人都可以学游泳。 Can anybody come, or are there special invitations? 是任何人都可以来？还是要有特别邀请才可以？

*anyhow
/ˈenihaʊ ||; ˈɛnɪˌhaυ/adv
1 =ANYWAY
2 in a careless way; not arranged in any order 随便；杂乱无章: She threw the clothes down onto the bed, just anyhow. 她把衣服往床上乱扔。

*anyone
/ˈeniwʌn ||; ˈɛnɪˌwʌn/ =ANYBODY

anyplace
/ˈenipleɪs ||; ˈɛnɪˌples/ (US 美) =ANYWHERE

*anything
/ˈeniθɪŋ ||; ˈɛnɪˌθɪŋ/pronoun
1 (usually in negative sentences and in questions 通常用于否定句及疑问句) one thing (of any kind) （任何事物的）一个: It was so dark that I couldn't see anything at all. 太黑了，我根本什么都看不见。 There isn't anything interesting in the newspaper today. 今天报上没什么吸引人的东西。 Did you buy anything? 你买了什么东西吗？ ‘I'd like a kilo of apples please.’ ‘ Anything else?’ (= any other thing?) “我想要一公斤苹果。”“还要别的吗？”
The difference between something and anything is the same as the difference between some and any. Look at the note at some. something 和 anything 之间的差别与 some 和 any 的差别一样。参看 some 的注释。
2 any thing or things: it does not matter what 任何事物（不管是什么）: I'm very hungry -- I'll eat anything! 我很饿，什么都吃得下！ I'll do anything you say. 你说的我都会照做。
anything but not at all 根本不；绝不: Their explanation was anything but clear. 他们的解释根本不清楚。 anything like sb/sth at all similar to sb/sth; nearly 与某人或某物相同、相像或差不多: She isn't anything like her sister, is she? 她一点也不像她姐姐，不是吗？ This car isn't anything like as fast as mine. 这辆车完全不及我那辆快。 as happy, quick, etc as anything(spoken 口语) very happy, quick, etc 很快乐；很快… like anything→LIKE² not come to anything→COME

*anyway
/ˈeniweɪ ||; ˈɛnɪˌwe/ (also anyhow) adv
1 (used to add an extra point or reason) in any case （用于补充说明）无论如何，不管怎么说: It's too late now, anyway. 无论如何现在已经太晚了。 I don't want to go out tonight, and anyway I haven't got any money. 我今晚不想出门，反正我也没有钱。 [SYN] besides 同义词为 besides
2 in spite of sth; even so 尽管；即使如此: I'm afraid I can't come to your party, but thanks anyway. 我恐怕不能出席你的酒会，不过还是谢谢你。
3 used after a pause in order to change the subject or go back to a subject being discussed before （用于停顿之后，以改变话题或回到先前讨论的话题）: Anyhow, that's enough about my problems. How are you? 好了，我的问题说够了，你呢？ Anyhow, as I was saying... 嗯，我刚才在说…
4 used to correct or slightly change what you have said （用于修正或稍稍改变刚说过的话）: He works in a bank. He did when I last saw him, anyway. 他在银行工作。至少我上次见他的时候是这样。

*anywhere
/ˈeniweə(r) ||; ˈɛnɪˌhwɛr/ (US also 美亦作 anyplace) adv
1 (usually in negative sentences or in questions 通常用于否定句或疑问句) in, at or to any place 在或去任何地方: I can't find my keys anywhere. 我到处找都找不到我的钥匙。 Is there a post office anywhere near here? 这里附近有没有邮政局？ You can't buy the book anywhere else (= in another place). 你在别处买不到这本书。
The difference between somewhere and anywhere is the same as the difference between some and any. Look at the note at some. somewhere 和 anywhere 之间的差别与 some 和 any 的差别一样。参看 some 的注释。
2 any place; it does not matter where 任何地方（不管什么地方）: You can sit anywhere you like. 你爱坐哪里就坐哪里。

AOB
/ˌeɪ əʊ ˈbi: ||; ˌe o ˈbi/abbr any other business (things that people need to discuss at the end of a meeting after everything on theAGENDA(= list of things to discuss)has been dealt with) 任何其他事情（议程上的事讨论完毕以后散会前还须要讨论的事）

/eɪˈɔ:tə ||; eˈɔrtə/noun [C] the mainARTERY(= tube)that carries blood from the heart to the rest of the body 主动脉 ☞picture at heart 见 heart 插图

*apart
/əˈpɑ:t ||; əˈpɑrt/adv
1 away from sb/sth or each other; not together 相距；分开: The doors slowly slid apart. 两扇门慢慢地各自滑开。 Stand with your feet apart. 叉开两脚站着。 The houses are ten metres apart. 两幢房子相隔十米。 I'm afraid our ideas are too far apart. 恐怕我们的想法相差太远了。
2 into pieces 成碎片；支离破碎: The material was so old that it just fell/came apart in my hands. 这物料实在太旧，我一拿到手上就支离破碎了。
take sth apart to separate sth into pieces 拆开某物: He took the whole bicycle apart. 他将整架自行车拆开。 tell A and B apart to see the difference between A and B 分辨（两者）: It's very difficult to tell the twins apart. 很难辨别那对孪生儿。

*aˈpart from
(especially US 尤为美 aside from) prep
1 except for 除…以外: I've answered all the questions apart from the last one. 除最后一道题以外，所有的题我都作答了。 There's nobody here apart from me. 这里除了我之外，没有别人。
2 as well as; in addition to 除了…还有: Apart from music, she also loves sport and reading. 除了音乐之外，她还喜爱体育运动和阅读。

*appeal¹
/əˈpi:l ||; əˈpil/verb[I]
1 appeal to sb (for sth);appeal for sth to make a serious request for sth you need or want very much 请求；恳求: Relief workers in the disaster area are appealing for more help and supplies. 灾区的救援人员呼吁各方多施以援手，提供更多物资。 She appealed to the kidnappers to let her son go. 她恳求绑架者释放她的儿子。
2 appeal (to sb) to be attractive or interesting to sb 吸引: The idea of living in the country doesn't appeal to me at all. 在乡间生活的想法一点也不令我感兴趣。
3 appeal to sth to influence sb's feelings or thoughts so that he/she will do sth you want 影响、激发某人的感情或思想: We aim to appeal to people's generosity. 我们希望能激发大家的慷慨之情。
4 appeal (against/for sth) to ask sb in authority to make or change a decision 请求掌权者作出或改变决定；上诉: He decided to appeal against his conviction. 他决定对自己的定罪上诉。 The player fell down and appealed for a penalty. 那球员跌倒在地，请求罚球。
*appeal²
/əˈpi:l ||; əˈpil/noun
1 [C] a serious request for sth you need or want very much 恳求；呼吁: The police have made an urgent appeal for witnesses to come forward. 警方已紧急呼吁目击者挺身而出。
2 [C] an appeal to sth a suggestion that tries to influence sb's feelings or thoughts so that he/she will do what you want 影响他人思想感情的建议；激发人的建议
3 [C] a formal request to sb in authority to change a decision 向掌权者建议改变决定的请求；上诉
4 [U] the attraction or interesting quality of sth/sb 吸引力；魅力

2 showing that you need help, etc 求助的；恳求的: an appealing look 求助的一瞥 ➔appealingly adv

*appear
/əˈpɪə(r) ||; əˈpɪr/verb
1 linking verb appear to be/do sth;appear (that)... to seem 看来；似乎: She appears to be very happy in her job. 她看来工作得很愉快。 It appears that you were given the wrong information. 看来你收到了错误的消息。 ☞adjective apparent 形容词为 apparent
2 [I] to suddenly be seen; to come into sight 出现: The bus appeared from round the corner. 那辆公共汽车从转角处出现了。 [OPP] disappear 反义词为 disappear
3 [I] to begin to exist 开始存在: The disease is thought to have appeared in Africa. 相信那种疾病是在非洲出现的。
4 [I] to be published or printed 刊出；出版；发表: The article appeared in this morning's paper. 那篇文章刊载于今天上午的报纸上。
5 [I] to perform or speak where you are seen by a lot of people 在公众场合表演或演说: to appear on television/in a play 在电视上亮相；在戏剧中演出

*appearance

*apply
/əˈplaɪ ||; əˈplaɪ/verb (present participle applying third person singular present applies;past tense past participle applied)
1 [I] apply (to sb) (for sth) to ask for sth in writing （以书面）申请: I've applied to that company for a job. 我已经向那家公司申请工作。 She's applying for a place at university. 她正在申请上大学。
2 [I] apply (to sb/sth) to concern or involve sb/sth 关于；适用于: This information applies to all children born after 1997. 这个消息关乎所有1997年以后出世的孩子。
3 [T] apply sth (to sth) to make practical use of sth 应用: new technology which can be applied to solving problems in industry 可用来解决工业难题的新技术
4 [T] (usually passive 通常用于被动语态) to use a word, a name, etc to describe sb/sth 称；称呼: I don't think the term ‘music’ can be applied to that awful noise. 我认为那种难听的噪音不能称为“音乐”。
5 [T] apply sth (to sth) to put or spread sth onto sth 敷；涂: Apply the cream to the infected area twice a day. 将软膏涂在受感染的地方，每日两次。
6 [T] apply yourself/sth (to sth/doing sth) to make yourself give all your attention to sth 集中精力；专注: to apply your mind to sth 专心致力于某事

2 [C] a job or a position of responsibility 职位；职务: a temporary/permanent appointment 临时／固定的职位

*appreciate
/əˈpri:ʃieɪt ||; əˈpriʃɪˌet/verb
1 [T] to enjoy sth or to understand the value of sb/sth 欣赏；鉴赏；赏识: My boss doesn't appreciate me. 老板不赏识我。 I don't appreciate good coffee -- it all tastes the same to me. 好咖啡我品尝不出来，对我来说都是一个味道。
2 [T] to understand a problem, situation, etc （对问题、情况等）了解: I appreciate your problem but I'm afraid I can't help you. 我了解你的问题，但恐怕帮不了你的忙。
3 [T] to be grateful for sth 感激: Thanks very much. I really appreciate your help. 多谢。我很感激你帮忙。
4 [I] to increase in value 增值；升值

appreciation
/əˌpri:ʃiˈeɪʃn ||; əˌpriʃɪˈeʃən/noun
1 [U] understanding and enjoyment of the value of sth 欣赏；鉴赏；赏识: I'm afraid I have little appreciation of modern architecture. 我恐怕欣赏不了现代建筑。
2 [U] the feeling of being grateful for sth 感激；感谢: We bought him a present to show our appreciation for all the work he had done. 我们买了一份礼物送给他，对他出力表示感谢。
3 [U] [sing] understanding of a situation, problem, etc （对情况、问题等的）明白，了解
4 [U] [sing] an increase in value 增值；升值

appreciative
/əˈpri:ʃətɪv ||; əˈpriʃɪˌetɪv/adj
1 feeling or showing pleasure or admiration 赞赏的；欣赏的；钦羡的: an appreciative audience 懂得欣赏的听众
2 appreciative (of sth) grateful for sth 感激的: He was very appreciative of our efforts to help. 他很感激我们出力帮忙。

apprehend
/ˌæprɪˈhend ||; ˌæprɪˈhɛnd/verb [T] (formal 正式) (used about the police 指警察) to catch sb and arrest him/her 把某人捉拿归案；逮捕

apprehensive
/ˌæprɪˈhensɪv ||; ˌæprɪˈhɛnsɪv/adj worried or afraid that sth unpleasant may happen 担忧的；恐惧的: I'm feeling apprehensive about tomorrow's exam. 我对明天的考试感到担忧。 ➔apprehension /-ʃn ||; -ʃən/ noun [C,U]

apprentice
/əˈprentɪs ||; əˈprɛntɪs/noun [C] a person who works for low pay, in order to learn the skills needed in a particular job 学徒: an apprentice electrician/chef/plumber 电工／厨师／管子工学徒

apprenticeship
/əˈprentɪʃɪp ||; əˈprɛntɪˌʃɪp/noun [C,U] the state or time of being an apprentice 学徒身分；学徒期: He served a two-year apprenticeship as a carpenter. 他当了两年木匠学徒。

*approach¹
/əˈprəʊtʃ ||; əˈprotʃ/verb
1 [I,T] to come near or nearer to sb/sth 临近；逼近；接近: The day of the exam approached. 考试的日期临近了。 When you approach the village you will see a garage on your left. 你走近那个村子就会见到左边有个修车厂。
2 [T] to begin to deal with a problem, a situation, etc 着手处理: What is the best way to approach this problem? 着手处理这个难题最好的方法是什么？
3 [T] to speak to sb usually in order to ask for sth 找某人接洽或商量: I'm going to approach my bank manager about a loan. 我打算为贷款的事与银行经理接洽。
approach²
/əˈprəʊtʃ ||; əˈprotʃ/noun
1 [C] a way of dealing with sb/sth 途径；门路；方法: Parents don't always know what approach to take with teenage children. 父母往往不知道怎样对待十多岁的子女。
2 [sing] the act of coming nearer (to sb/sth) 接近；走近: the approach of winter 冬天临近
3 [C] a request for sth 请求: The company has made an approach to us for financial assistance. 那家公司请求我们给予财政支持。
4 [C] a road or path leading to sth 路径；通道: the approach to the village 通向那个村落的路

approachable
/əˈprəʊtʃəbl ||; əˈprotʃəbḷ/adj
1 friendly and easy to talk to 可亲近的；平易近人的
2 (not before a noun 不用于名词前) that can be reached 可以到达 [SYN] accessible 同义词为 accessible

*appropriate¹
/əˈprəʊpriət ||; əˈproprɪɪt/adj appropriate (for/to sth) suitable or right for a particular situation, person, use, etc 适合的；适当的: The matter will be dealt with by the appropriate authorities. 会有适当的官员来处理那件事。 I don't think this film is appropriate for children. 我认为这部电影不适合儿童观看。 [OPP] inappropriate 反义词为 inappropriate ➔appropriately adv
appropriate²
/əˈprəʊprieɪt ||; əˈproprɪˌet/verb [T] (formal 正式) to take sth to use for yourself, usually without permission 私占；挪用；擅用: He appropriated the money from the company's pension fund. 他挪用了公司养老基金的钱。 ➔appropriation /əˌprəʊpriˈeɪʃn ||; əˌproprɪˈeʃən/ noun [U] [sing]

*approval
/əˈpru:vl ||; əˈpruvḷ/noun [U] feeling, showing or saying that you think sth is good; agreement 赞成；同意；嘉许: Everybody gave their approval tothe proposal. 人人都赞成那个提议。

*approve
/əˈpru:v ||; əˈpruv/verb
1 [I] approve (of sb/sth) to be pleased about sth; to like sb/sth 满意；喜欢: His father didn't approve of him becoming a dancer. 他父亲不赞成他当舞蹈演员。 Her parents don't approve of her friends. 她父母不喜欢她的朋友。 [OPP] disapprove 反义词为 disapprove
2 [T] to agree formally to sth or to say that sth is correct 批准；核准；认可: We need to get an accountant to approve these figures. 我们须要找会计师核准这些数字。

approving
/əˈpru:vɪŋ ||; əˈpruvɪŋ/adj showing support or admiration for sth 表示认可、支持或赞赏的: ‘Good,’ he said with an approving smile. “很好，”他脸上露出赞许的笑容说。 ➔approvingly adv

approx.
abbr (written 书面语) approximate; approximately 大约；大概

*approximate
/əˈprɒksɪmət ||; əˈprɑksəmət/adj almost correct but not completely accurate 差不多的；大概的；接近的: The approximate time of arrival is 3 o'clock. 抵达时间大约是3点。 I can only give you an approximate idea of the cost. 价钱方面，我只能跟你说个约数。

*approximately
/əˈprɒksɪmətli ||; əˈprɑksəˌmətlɪ/adv about; roughly 大约: It's approximately fifty miles from here. 离这里大约五十英里。

approximation
/əˌprɒksɪˈmeɪʃn ||; əˌprɑksəˈmeʃən/noun [C] a number, answer, etc which is nearly, but not exactly, right 约数；近似的答案；概算

ˌApril ˈFool's Day
noun [sing] 1 April 愚人节（4月1日） On this day it is traditional for people to play tricks on each other, especially by inventing silly stories and trying to persuade other people that they are true. If somebody believes such a story he/she is called an April Fool. 根据传统，4月1日是彼此愚弄的日子，尤其是瞎编故事骗人，并设法让别人信以为真。被愚弄的人叫做 April Fool。

arch¹
/ɑ:tʃ ||; ɑrtʃ/noun[C]

*area
/ˈeəriə ||; ˈɛrɪə/noun
1 [C] a part of a town, a country or the world 地区: Housing is very expensive in the Tokyo area. 东京地区的房屋非常昂贵。 The wettest areas are in the West of the country. 最潮湿的地区在那个国家西部。 built-up areas (= where there are a lot of buildings) 建筑物林立的地区 Forests cover a large area of the country. 该国大片地区为森林覆盖。 ☞Look at the note at district. 参看 district 的注释。
2 [C,U] the size of a surface, that you can calculate by multiplying the length by the width 面积: The area of the office is 35 square metres. 办公室的面积是35平方米。 The office is 35 square metres in area. 办公室的面积是35平方米。 ☞Look at volume. 参看 volume。
3 [C] a space used for a particular activity 作特别用途的空间: The restaurant has a non-smoking area. 那家餐厅有禁烟区。
4 [C] a particular part of a subject or activity （课题或活动的）一部份，方面: Training is one area of the business that we could improve. 培训工作是我们公司的业务有待改进的地方。

arena
/əˈri:nə ||; əˈrinə/noun[C]
1 an area with seats around it where public entertainments (sporting events, concerts, etc) are held （四周有座位的）表演场，竞技场
2 an area of activity that concerns the public 公众活动场所

arguable
/ˈɑ:gjuəbl ||; ˈɑrgjυəbḷ/adj
1 probably true; that you can give reasons for 可争辩的；可论证的: It is arguable that all hospital treatment should be free. 住院治疗应全部免费或许是有道理的。
2 probably not true; that you can give reasons against 不一定正确的；可提出质疑的；可疑的 ➔arguably /-əbli ||; -əblɪ/ adv ‘King Lear’ is arguably Shakespeare's best play. 《李尔王》可以说是莎士比亚最好的剧作。

*argue
/ˈɑ:gju: ||; ˈɑrgju/verb
1 [I] argue (with sb) (about/over sth) to say things, often angrily that show that you do not agree with sb about sth （与人）争辩，争吵，理论: The couple next door are always arguing. 邻家那对夫妇老是吵嘴。 I never argue with my husband about money. 我从不为钱与丈夫争吵。 ☞Look at fight ¹(4) and quarrel ². 参看 fight^1(4)及 quarrel^2。
2 [I,T] argue that...;argue (for/against sth) to give reasons that support your opinion about sth （就某事）论证，争辩: He argued against buying a new computer. 他提出理由反对买新计算机。

*argument
/ˈɑ:gjumənt ||; ˈɑrgjəmənt/noun
1 [C,U] an argument (with sb) (about/over sth) an angry discussion between two or more people who disagree with each other 争论；争吵: Sue had an argument with her father about politics. 休和父亲为了政治问题而争论。 He accepted the decision without argument. 他没有争辩就接受了决定。 ☞A quarrel is usually about something less serious. quarrel 通常指争论不那么严重的问题。
2 [C] the reason(s) that you give to support your opinion about sth 论据；理由: What are the arguments for/against lower taxes? 有什么理由赞成／反对降低赋税？

argumentative
/ˌɑ:gjuˈmentətɪv ||; ˌɑrgjəˈmɛntətɪv/adj often involved in or enjoying arguments 好争论的

aria
/ˈɑ:riə ||; ˈɑrɪə/noun [C] a song for one voice, especially in an opera 咏叹调，独唱曲（尤指歌剧中的）

/ˈærɪd ||; ˈærɪd/adj (used about land or climate) very dry; with little or no rain （指土地或气候）干旱的，干燥的

/əˈraɪz ||; əˈraɪz/verb [I] (past tense arose /əˈrəʊz ||; əˈroz/ past participle arisen /əˈrɪzn ||; əˈrɪzṇ/) to begin to exist; to appear 开始存在；出现: If any problems arise, let me know. 如果出现问题，请告诉我。

arithmetic
/əˈrɪθmətɪk ||; əˈrɪθməˌtɪk/noun [U] (mathematics数学) the kind of mathematics which involves counting with numbers (adding, subtracting, multiplying and dividing) 算术: I'm not very good at mental arithmetic. 我不大善于心算。

arithˌmetic proˈgression
(also arithˌmetical proˈgression) noun [C] (mathematics数学) a series of numbers that decrease or increase by the same amount each time, for example 2, 4, 6, 8 算术级数，等差级数（每次以同样数量递减或递增的一系列数字，如2、4、6、8） ☞Compare geometric progression. 与geometric progression比较。

*arm¹
/ɑ:m ||; ɑrm/noun[C]
1 the long part at each side of your body connecting your shoulder to your hand 臂；胳膊: He was carrying a newspaper under his arm. 他腋下挟着一份报纸。 ☞picture at body 见body插图
2 the part of a piece of clothing that covers your arm; a sleeve 衣袖: He had a hole in the arm of his jumper. 他的套头毛衣袖子穿了个洞。
3 the part of a chair where you rest your arms 椅子的扶手
arm in arm with your arm folded around sb else's arm 臂挽着臂: The two friends walked arm in arm. 两个朋友挽臂而行。 ☞picture on page S19 见S19页插图 cross/fold your arms to cross your arms in front of your chest 两臂交错放在胸前: She folded her arms and waited. 她双臂交叉在胸前等候。 James was sitting with his arms crossed. 詹姆斯坐着，双臂交叉在胸前。 ☞picture on page S19 见S19页插图 twist sb's arm→TWIST¹ with open arms→OPEN¹

*around
/əˈraʊnd ||; əˈraυnd/adv prep
1 (also about) in or to various places or directions 到处；四处: This is our office -- David will show you around(= show you the different parts of it). 这是我们的办公室，戴维会带你四处看看。 They wandered around the town, looking at the shops. 他们在城中四处逛商店。
2 moving so as to face in the opposite direction 向相反方向移动；回转: Turn around and go back the way you came. 转身往来时的路走。
3 on all sides; forming a circle 四周；形成一圈: The park has a wall all around. 公园的四周有围墙。 Gather around so that you can all see. 围拢过来，好让你们都看得到。 We sat down around the table. 我们围着桌子坐下。 In senses
1,
2 and
3 round can be used instead of around. 用于第
1、
2及
3义时 round 可取代 around。
4 near a place 附近: Is there is a bank around here? 附近有没有银行？
5 (also about) present or available 在；找得到: I went to the house but there was nobody around. 我到那所房子去，但里面没有人。
6 (also about) approximately 大约；左右: I'll see you around seven(= at about 7 o'clock). 我们七点左右见。
7 (also about) used for activities with no real purpose （用于没有明确目的的活动）: ‘What are you doing?’ ‘Nothing, just lazing around.’ “你在做什么？”“没什么，只是闲散度日而已。”

/əˈraʊz ||; əˈraυz/verb [T] to cause a particular reaction in people 引起反应；激起: to arouse sb's curiosity/interest 引起某人的好奇／兴趣 ➔arousal noun [U]

/ɑ:ˈpedʒiəʊ ||; ɑrˈpɛdʒɪˌo/noun [C] (plural arpeggios) (used in music 用于音乐) a group of notes which are played quickly one after the other 琶音 ☞Compare chord. 与 chord 比较。

*arrange
/əˈreɪndʒ ||; əˈrendʒ/verb
1 [T] to put sth in order or in a particular pattern 排列；整理: The books were arranged in alphabetical order. 那些书按英文字母顺序排列。 Arrange the chairs in a circle. 将椅子围成一圈。 She arranged the flowers in a vase. 她把花插在花瓶里。
2 [I,T] arrange (for) sth;arrange to do sth;arrange (sth) with sb to make plans and preparations so that sth can happen in the future 筹备；安排: We're arranging a surprise party for Aisha. 我们在为艾莎安排一个惊喜聚会。 She arranged to meet Stuart after work. 她约好下班后去见斯图尔特。 She arranged for her mother to look after the baby. 她安排母亲照看婴儿。

arˌranged ˈmarriage
noun [C] a marriage in which the parents choose the husband or wife for their child 父母作主的婚姻

*arrangement
/əˈreɪndʒmənt ||; əˈrendʒmənt/noun
1 [C] [usu.pl] plans or preparations for sth that will happen in the future 安排；筹备: Come round this evening and we'll make arrangements for the party. 你今晚过来，我们为聚会做筹备工作。
2 [C,U] an agreement with sb to do sth 约定；协议；商定: They have an arrangement to share the cost of the food. 他们商议好如何分摊食物的费用。 We both need to use the computer so we'll have to come to some arrangement. 我们俩都要用那台计算机，所以我们得达成某种协议。
3 [C] a group of things that have been placed in a particular pattern 排列或整理好的事物: a flower arrangement 插好的花

array
/əˈreɪ ||; əˈre/noun [C] a large collection of things, especially one that is impressive and is seen by other people 陈列；展示

arrears
/əˈrɪəz ||; əˈrɪrz/noun [pl] money that sb owes that he/she should have paid earlier （逾期未付的）欠款 be in arrears;fall/get into arrears to be late in paying money that you owe 拖欠款子: I'm in arrears with the rent. 我欠了租金未缴。 be paid in arrears to be paid for work after you have done the work 完工后付给工资: You will be paid monthly in arrears. 你的工资每月月底支付。

*arrival
/əˈraɪvl ||; əˈraɪvḷ/noun
1 [C,U] reaching the place to which you were travelling 到达，抵达（目的地）: On our arrival we were told that our rooms had not been reserved. 我们到达目的地，才知道没有预留房间给我们。
2 [C] people or things that have arrived 到达的人或物: We brought in extra chairs for the late arrivals. 我们为迟到者搬来额外的椅子。

*arrive
/əˈraɪv ||; əˈraɪv/verb[I]
1 arrive (at/in...) to reach the place to which you were travelling 到达，抵达（目的地）: We arrived home at about midnight. 我们大约午夜到家。 What time does the train arrive in Newcastle? 列车什么时候到达纽卡斯尔？ They arrived at the station ten minutes late. 他们晚了十分钟到达车站。
Be careful. We use arrive in with the name of a town, country, etc and arrive at with a place, building, etc 注意：到达某个有具体名字的城镇、国家等用 arrive in，到达某个地方、建筑物等用 arrive at。
2 to come or happen 来到；发生: The day of the wedding had finally arrived. 婚礼的日子终于到了。
arrive at to reach sth 达成: We finally arrived at a decision. 我们终于作出了决定。

*art
/ɑ:t ||; ɑrt/noun
1 [U] the activity or skill of producing things such as paintings, designs, etc; the objects that are produced 美术；艺术；艺术作品: an art class 美术班 modern art 现代艺术 I've never been good at art. 我的美术从来不行。 ☞Look at work of art. 参看 work of art。

We usually contrast arts (or arts subjects) with sciences (or science subjects). 文科 (arts) 或文科科目 (arts subjects) 通常相对于理科 (sciences) 或理科科目 (science subjects) 而言。

arthropod
/ˈɑ:θrəpɒd ||; ˈɑrθrəˌpɑd/noun [C] any of the PHYLUM (= group)of animals that have a hard body without a BACKBONE in it. *as
/əz;strong form æz ||; əz; æz/ conj prep adv
1 while sth else is happening 同一时候；当时: The phone rang just as I was leaving the house. 我刚要出门，电话就响起来了。 As she walked along the road, she thought about her father. 她沿着那条路走着，心里想着她父亲。
2 as... as used for comparing people or things （用于比较人或事物）: Todor's almost as tall as me. 托多尔差不多跟我一样高。 Todor's almost as tall as I am. 托多尔差不多跟我一样高。 It's not as cold as it was yesterday. 今天没有昨天那么冷。 I'd like an appointment as soon as possible. 我希望能尽早预约一个时间。 She earns twice as much as her husband. 她赚的钱比她丈夫多一倍。 I haven't got as many books as you have. 我的书没有你那样多。
3 used for talking about sb/sth's job, role or function （用于指工作、身分或作用）: He works as a train driver. 他当火车司机。 Think of me as your friend, not as your boss. 不要把我当作上司，把我视为朋友好了。 You could use this white sheet as a tablecloth. 你可以用这条白床单当桌布。
4 in a particular way, state, etc; like 以某种方式或状态等: Please do as I tell you. 请照我的话做。 Leave the room as it is. Don't move anything. 让房间保持原状。什么也别动。
5 used at the beginning of a comment about what you are saying （用于带出要说的话）: As you know, I've decided to leave at the end of the month. 大家都知道，我已经决定月底离开。
6 because 因为: I didn't buy the dress, as I decided it was too expensive. 我没有买那件衣服，因为我认为太贵了。
as for used when you are starting to talk about a different person or thing （用于改谈另一人或另一事物）: Gianni's upstairs. As for Andreas, I've no idea where he is. 詹尼在楼上。至于安德烈亚斯，我不知道他在哪里。 as if;as though used for saying how sb/sth appears （用于描述样子）: She looks as if/though she's just got out of bed. 她好像刚起床的样子。 as it were used for saying that sth is only true in a certain way （用于表示某事物只在某方面正确）: She felt, as it were, a stranger in her own house. 她觉得，她在家中有些像个外人。 as of;as from starting from a particular time 自某时刻开始: As from next week, Tim Shaw will be managing this department. 从下个星期开始，蒂姆˙肖将管理这个部门。 as to about a particular thing; concerning 关于某事物: I was given no instructions as to how to begin. 对于如何开始，没有人给我指示。

*ask
/ɑ:sk ||; æsk/verb
1 [I,T] ask (sb) (about sb/sth);ask sb sth to put a question to sb in order to find out some information 问: We need to ask about tickets. 我们须要问一问票的事。 Can I ask you a question? 我能问你一个问题吗？ Ask him how old he is. 问问他有多大年纪了。 She asked if I wanted tea or coffee. 她问我要喝茶还是喝咖啡。 ‘What's the time?’ he asked. 他问：“现在几点钟？” He asked what the time was. 他问什么时间了。 He asked me the time. 他问我时间。
2 [I,T] ask (sb) for sth;ask sth (of sb);ask sb to do sth to request that sb gives you sth or does sth for you 要求: She sat down and asked for a cup of coffee. 她坐下来，要了一杯咖啡。 Don't ask Joe for money -- he hasn't got any. 别向乔借钱，他没有钱。 You are asking too much of him -- he can't possibly do all that! 你对他的要求太高了，那么多事情他不可能全做得来！ Ring this number and ask for Mrs Khan. 拨这个号码，找卡恩太太听电话。 I asked him if he would drive me home. 我问他可不可以开车送我回家。 I asked him to drive me home. 我叫他开车送我回家。
3 [I,T] to request permission to do sth 请求准许: I'm sure she'll let you go if you ask. 我敢肯定，如果你提出请求，她会让你走。 He asked to use our phone. 他要求借用我们的电话。 We asked if we could go home early. 我们问是否允许我们早点回家。
4 [T] ask sb (to sth) to invite sb 邀请
5 [T] to say the price that you want for sth 索价；开价: How much are they asking for their car? 那辆汽车他们索价多少？
ask for trouble/it to behave in a way that will almost certainly cause you problems 招惹麻烦；自找麻烦: Driving when you're tired is just asking for trouble. 疲劳时开车根本是自找麻烦。 if you ask me if you want my opinion 如果你想听听我的意见；要我说；恕我直言 ask after sb to ask about sb's health or to ask for news of sb 问候；问安: Tina asked after you today. 蒂娜今天问候过你。

*at
/ət;strong form æt ||; ət; æt/prep
1 used to show where sb/sth is or where sth happens （用于表示位置或地点）: at the bottom/top of the page 在页的下端／上端 He was standing at the door. 他站在门口。 Change trains at Chester. 在切斯特转车。 We were at home all weekend. 我们整个周末都在家里。 Are the children at school? 孩子们都就学吗？ ‘Where's Peter?’ ‘He's at Sue's.’ (= at Sue's house) “彼得在哪里？”“在休家里。”
2 used to show when sth happens （用于表示时间）: I start work at 9 o'clock. 我9点钟开始工作。 at the weekend 在周末 at night 在晚上 at Easter 在复活节 She got married at 18 (= when she was 18). 她18岁结婚。
3 in the direction of sb/sth 面向；朝着；对着: What are you looking at? 你在看什么？ He pointed a gun at the policeman. 他用枪对着那名警察。 Don't shout at me! 不要向我吆喝！
4 because of sth 因为；由于: I was surprised at her behaviour. 她的行为使我吃惊。 We laughed at his jokes. 他的笑话引得我们都笑起来。
5 used to show what sb is doing or what is happening （用于表示某人正在做什么或正在发生的事情）: They were hard at work. 他们在努力工作。 The two countries were at war. 两国处于交战状态。
6 used to show the price, rate, speed, etc of sth （用于表示价格、比率、速度等）: We were travelling at about 50 miles per hour. 我们当时以每小时约50英里的速度前进。
7 used with adjectives that show how well sb/sth does sth （用于与形容词连用，表示程度）: She's not very good at French. 她的法语不大好。

*attach

*attack¹
/əˈtæk ||; əˈtæk/noun

3 [C] a short period when you suffer badly from a disease, medical condition, etc 病发；（疾病等的）侵袭: an attack of asthma/flu/nerves 哮喘病／感冒／神经质的发作
4 [C] the act of trying to score a point in a game of sport （体育比赛中）发动攻势，进攻
*attack²
/əˈtæk ||; əˈtæk/verb
1 [I,T] to try to hurt or defeat sb/sth by using force 攻击；进攻: The child was attacked by a dog. 孩子受到狗的袭击。
2 [T] to say strongly that you do not like or agree with sb/sth 抨击: Steffi attacked Guy's right-wing political views. 斯蒂菲抨击盖伊的右派政治观点。
3 [T] to damage or harm sb/sth 伤害: a virus that attacks the nervous system 破坏神经系统的病毒
4 [I,T] to try to score a point in a game of sport （体育比赛中）发动攻势，进攻: This team attacks better than it defends. 这个队的进攻比防守出色。

2 [C] a skill or sth you have achieved 技能；成就；造诣

*attempt¹
/əˈtempt ||; əˈtɛmpt/verb [T] attempt (to do) sth to try to do sth that is difficult 尝试，设法（做困难的事）；企图: She was accused of attempted murder(= she tried to murder sb but did not succeed). 她被控意图谋杀。 Don't attempt to make him change his mind. 别想使他改变主意。
*attempt²
/əˈtempt ||; əˈtɛmpt/noun[C]
1 an attempt (to do sth/at doing sth) an act of trying to do sth 尝试；试图: The thief made no attempt to run away. 窃贼并未试图逃跑。 I failed the exam once but passed at the second attempt. 我考试第一次不及格，但第二次尝试就及格了。 They failed in their attemptto reach the North Pole. 他们试图到达北极，但失败了。
2 an attempt (on sb/sth) trying to attack or beat sb/sth 试图攻击或击败: an attempt on sb's life (= to kill sb) 试图杀害某人
a last-ditch attempt→LAST¹

*attend
/əˈtend ||; əˈtɛnd/verb
1 [T] to go to or be present at a place 出席；参加: Do you attend church regularly? 你经常上教堂吗？ The children attend the local school. 孩子们在区内的学校上学。
2 [I] (formal 正式)attend to sb/sth to give your care, thought or attention to sb/sth or look after sb/sth 照顾；注意；照料: Please attend to this matter immediately. 请立即处理这件事。

attendance
/əˈtendəns ||; əˈtɛndəns/noun
1 [U] being present somewhere 出席；参加: Attendance at lectures is compulsory. 讲课是硬性规定要出席的。
2 [C,U] the number of people who go to or are present at a place 出席人数；参加人数: There was a poor attendance at the meeting. 出席会议的人寥寥无几。

attendant¹
/əˈtendənt ||; əˈtɛndənt/noun [C] a person whose job is to serve or help people in a public place （公共场所的）服务员，管理员: a car park attendant 停车场管理员
attendant²
/əˈtendənt ||; əˈtɛndənt/adj (only before a noun 只用于名词前) (formal 正式) that goes together with or results from sth 伴随的；附带的: unemployment and all its attendant social problems 失业及其连带的所有社会问题

*attention¹
/əˈtenʃn ||; əˈtɛnʃən/noun [U]:
1 watching, listening to or thinking about sb/sth carefully 注意；留心；关注: I shouted in order to attract her attention. 我大声叫喊，希望引起她的注意。 Shy people hate to be the centre of attention (= the person that everybody is watching). 腼腆的人不喜欢成为大家注意的中心。 to hold sb's attention (= to keep them interested in sth) 吸引住某人
2 special care or action 护理；料理；照料: The hole in the roof needs urgent attention. 屋顶上的洞急需修补。 to require medical attention 需要医疗护理
3 a position in which a soldier stands up straight and still 立正: to stand/come to attention 立正
catch sb's attention/eye→CATCH¹ draw (sb's) attention to sth→DRAW¹ pay attention→PAY¹
attention²
/əˈtenʃn ||; əˈtɛnʃən/ exclamation used for asking people to listen to sth carefully （用于促请他人留心听）各位请注意

attentive
/əˈtentɪv ||; əˈtɛntɪv/adj attentive (to sb/sth) watching, listening to or thinking about sb/sth carefully 留心的；注意的；关注的: The hotel staff were very attentive to our needs. 那家酒店的职员对我们的需求考虑得很周到。 [OPP] inattentive 反义词为 inattentive ➔attentively adv to listen attentively to sth 留心听某事

attest
/əˈtest ||; əˈtɛst/verb [I,T] (formal 正式)
1 attest (to sth) to show that sth is true 证明，表明（某事是真的）: Her long fight against cancer attested to her courage. 她长期跟癌症作斗争，这证明了她的勇气。
2 to state that you believe that sth is true or genuine, for example in a court of law 为某事物的真实性作证（比如在法庭上）: The signature was attested by two witnesses. 有两名证人证明这签名是真的。

attrition
/əˈtrɪʃn ||; əˈtrɪʃən/noun [U]:
1 (formal 正式) a process of making sb/sth, especially your enemy, weaker by attacking him/her/it or causing problems for him/her/it over a period of time 消耗，削弱（敌人的力量）: It was a war of attrition. 这是一场消耗战。

*authority
/ɔ:ˈθɒrəti ||; ɔˈθɑrətɪ/noun (plural authorities)
1 [U] the power and right to give orders and make others obey 权力；权威；权势: Children often begin to question their parents' authority at a very early age. 儿童往往小小年纪就开始质疑父母的权威。 You must get this signed by a person in authority (= who has a position of power). 你必须请有关方面的负责人签署这份文件。
2 [U] authority (to do sth) the right or permission to do sth 权利；许可: The police have the authority to question anyone they wish. 警方有权随意查问任何人。 He was sacked for using a company vehicle without authority. 他因未经允许就使用公司车辆而被解雇。
3 [C] (often plural 常用复数) a person, group or government department that has the power to give orders, make official decisions, etc 有权力的人、团体或政府部门；掌权者；当局: I have to report this to the authorities. 我得把这件事向当局报告。
4 [U] a quality that sb has which makes it possible to influence and control other people 威信；影响力: He spoke with authority and everybody listened. 他说话很有威信，人人都留心听。
5 [C] an authority (on sth) a person with special knowledge 有专门知识的人；权威: He's an authority on criminal law. 他是刑法的权威。

*automatic¹

*average¹
/ˈævərɪdʒ ||; ˈævərɪdʒ/noun
1 [C] the number you get when you add two or more figures together and then divide the total by the number of figures you added 平均数；平均值: The average of 14, 3 and 1 is 6(= 18 divided by 3 is 6). 14、3和1的平均数是6。 He has scored 93 goals at an average of 1.55 per game. 他总共踢进93个球，平均每场踢进1.55个。
2 [U] the normal standard, amount or quality 通常的标准；一般水平；平均 [sing] On average, I buy a newspaper about twice a week. 我平均每周大约买两次报纸。
*average²

2 normal or typical 一般的；平常的: children of above / below averageintelligence 智力高于／低于一般水平的儿童
average³
/ˈævərɪdʒ ||; ˈævərɪdʒ/verb [T] to do, get, etc a certain amount as an average 以…作为平均数计算；平均为…: If we average 50 miles an hour we should arrive at about 4 o'clock. 如果我们以平均每小时50英里计算，我们当可在4点钟左右到达。 average out (at sth) to result in an average (of sth) 得出平均数

*awake²
/əˈweɪk ||; əˈwek/adj (not before a noun 不用于名词前) not sleeping 醒着: I was sleepy this morning but I'm wide awake now. 今天上午我很困，但现在我完全醒了。 They were so tired that they found it difficult to stay awake. 他们实在太累了，很难保持清醒。 I hope our singing didn't keep you awakelast night. 但愿我们昨晚唱歌没有使得你睡不着。 [OPP] asleep 反义词为 asleep

awake¹
/əˈweɪk ||; əˈwek/verb (past tense awoke /əˈwəʊk ||; əˈwok/ past participle awoken /əˈwəʊkən ||; əˈwokən/) [I,T] to wake up; to make sb/sth wake up 醒来；唤醒: I awoke to find that it was already 9 o'clock. 我醒来时，已经9点。 A sudden loud noise awoke us. 突如其来的一声巨响把我们吵醒了。 ☞ Wake up is more common than awake. wake up 较 awake 常用。

awaken
/əˈweɪkən ||; əˈwekən/verb
1 [I,T] (written 书面语) to wake up; to make sb/sth wake up 醒来；唤醒: We were awakened by a loud knock at the door. 敲门声很大，把我们吵醒了。 ☞ Wake up is much more common than awaken. wake up 较 awaken 常用得多。
2 [T] (formal 正式) to produce a particular feeling, attitude, etc in sb 唤起特定的感受、态度等: The film awakened memories of her childhood. 那部电影勾起她的童年回忆。
awaken sb to sth to make sb notice or realize sth for the first time 使注意或意识到；使发觉；使领悟: The letter awakened me to the seriousness of the situation. 我看了信，才知道事态严重。

awakening
/əˈweɪkənɪŋ ||; əˈwekənɪŋ/noun[sing]
1 the act of starting to feel or understand sth; the start of a feeling, etc 开始感到或理解；觉醒；萌生: the awakening of an interest in the opposite sex 开始对异性产生兴趣
2 a moment when sb notices or realizes sth for the first time 首次注意到或觉醒的时刻: It was a rude (= unpleasant) awakening when I suddenly found myself unemployed. 我突然发觉自己失业了，心里真不好受。

*award¹
/əˈwɔ:d ||; əˈwɔrd/noun[C]

2 an amount of money given to sb as the result of a court decision 据法庭裁定而支付的一笔钱；裁定额: She received an award of £5000 for damages. 她获判给损害赔偿金5000英镑。
*award²
/əˈwɔ:d ||; əˈwɔrd/verb [T] award sth (to sb) to give sth to sb as a prize, payment, etc 奖励；给予；判给（赔偿）: She was awarded first prize in the gymnastics competition. 她在体操比赛中得到第一名。 The court awarded £10000 each to the workers injured in the accident. 法院裁定在意外事故中受伤的工人每人可获赔偿10000英镑。

*aware
/əˈweə(r) ||; əˈwɛr/adj
1 aware (of sb/sth);aware (that) knowing about or realizing sth; conscious of sb/sth 意识到；知悉: I am well aware of the problems you face. 我很了解你面临的问题。 I suddenly became aware that someone was watching me. 我突然察觉到有人在注意我。 There is no other entrance, as far as I am aware. 据我所知，没有别的入口。 [OPP] unaware 反义词为 unaware
2 interested and informed 对…感兴趣而且有认识: Many young people are very politically aware. 许多年轻人很关心政治。

awareness
/əˈweənəs ||; əˈwɛrnɪs/noun [U] knowledge, consciousness or interest 知识；意识；兴趣: People's awareness of healthy eating has increased in recent years. 近年来人们对健康饮食的认识提高了。

awash
/əˈwɒʃ ||; əˈwɑʃ/adj (not before a noun 不用于名词前) awash (with sth) covered with water; flooded 浸水；被淹没 (figurative 比喻) The city was awash with rumours. 城里谣言四起。

*away
/əˈweɪ ||; əˈwe/adv adj ☞Look also at phrasal verbs, for example give away, take away. 另参看 give away、take away等短语动词。
1 away (from sb/sth) to a different place or in a different direction 到别处；朝别的方向: Go away! I'm busy! 走开！我忙得很！ I asked him a question, but he just looked away. 我问他一个问题，他却把目光移开了。
2 away (from sth) at a particular distance from a place 在某距离处: The village is two miles away from the sea. 那个村落离海两英里。 My parents live five minutes away. 我双亲的住处离这儿有五分钟路程。
3 away (from sth) (used about people) not present; absent （指人）不在: My neighbours are away on holiday at the moment. 我的邻居目前在别处度假。 Aki was away from school for two weeks with measles. 阿基出痲疹，两个星期没有上学。
4 in the future 在将来: Our summer holiday is only three weeks away. 再过三个星期我们就放暑假。
5 into a place where sth is usually kept 放进通常放置的地方: Put your books away now. 快把你的书收起来。 They cleared the dishes away (= off the table). 他们把碗碟从桌上收走。 Contrast throw sth away (= put it in the rubbish bin). 与 throw sth away 对比。
6 continuously, without stopping 持续；继续不断地: They chatted away for hours. 他们闲聊了好几个小时。
7 (used about a football, etc match) on the other team's ground （指足球赛等）在别队的场地: Our team's playing away on Saturday. 我们队星期六到别队的场地进行比赛。 an away match/game 作为客队的比赛 [OPP] (at) home 反义词为 (at) home
8 until sth disappears 直至完全消失: The crash of thunder slowly died away. 雷声渐渐消失。 He's given most of his money away. 他把自己大部份的钱给出去了。
do away with sb/sth to get rid of sb/sth 去掉；废除: The government are going to do away with the tax on fuel. 政府打算废除燃料税。 right/straight away immediately; without any delay 立即；马上: I'll phone the doctor right away. 我马上就打电话给医生。

awe
/ɔ: ||; ɔ/noun [U] feelings of respect and either fear or admiration 敬畏；敬慕: As a young boy he was very much in awe of his uncle. 小时候，他十分敬畏他叔叔。 be in awe of sb/sth to admire sb/sth and be slightly frightened of him/her/it 敬畏

ˈawe-inspiring
adj causing a feeling of respect and fear or admiration 令人敬畏或敬慕的

awesome
/ˈɔ:səm ||; ˈɔsəm/adj
1 impressive and sometimes frightening 给人深刻印象的（有时令人畏惧）: an awesome task 令人畏惧的任务

*awful
/ˈɔ:fl ||; ˈɔfḷ/adj
1 very bad or unpleasant 很坏的；令人不快的: We had an awful holiday. It rained every day. 我们的假期很糟糕，每天都下雨。 I feel awful -- I think I'll go to bed. 我觉得很不舒服，想去睡了。 What an awful thing to say! 竟说出这样的恶言恶语来！
2 terrible; very serious 可怕的；严重的: I'm afraid there's been some awful news. 恐怕有些坏消息呢。
3 (only before a noun 只用于名词前) (informal 非正式) very great 非常的: We've got an awful lot of work to do. 我们有一大堆的工作要做。

awfully
/ˈɔ:fli ||; ˈɔfḷɪ/adv (informal 非正式) very; very much 非常；极为: I'm awfully sorry. 我非常抱歉。

awkward
/ˈɔ:kwəd ||; ˈɔkwɚd/adj
1 difficult to deal with 很难处理的: That's an awkward question. 这是个很难回答的问题。 You've put me in an awkward position. 你使我的处境很尴尬。 an awkward customer 难以应付的顾客 The box isn't heavy but it's awkward to carry. 箱子不重，但很难拿。
2 not convenient, difficult 不方便的；困难的: My mother always phones at an awkward time. 我母亲总是在我不方便的时候打电话来。 This tin-opener is very awkward to clean. 这把开罐刀很难清洗。
3 embarrassed or embarrassing 困窘的；令人困窘的: I often feel awkward in a group of people. 我在人群中常常感到局促不安。 There was an awkward silence. 有一阵令人尴尬的沉默。
4 not using the body in the best way; not elegant or comfortable （身体姿势）别扭的、不雅观的或不舒服的: I was sitting with my legs in an awkward position. 我的两条腿没有坐舒服。 ➔awkwardly adv ➔awkwardness noun [U]

/ˈæksiəm ||; ˈæksɪəm/noun [C] a rule or principle that most people believe to be true 公理

axiomatic
/ˌæksiəˈmætɪk ||; ˌæksɪəˈmætɪk/adj (formal 正式) true in such an obvious way that you do not need evidence to show that it is true 自明的；公理的

axis
/ˈæksɪs ||; ˈæksɪs/noun [C] (plural axes /ˈæksi:z ||; ˈæksiz/)
1 a line we imagine through the middle of an object, around which the object turns 轴；轴线: The earth rotates on its axis. 地球绕地轴自转。 ☞picture at earth 见 earth 插图
2 a fixed line used for marking measurements on a diagram (graph) （图表上的）坐标，轴，参考轴线，基线: the horizontal/vertical axis 横／纵坐标轴

axle
/ˈæksl ||; ˈæksḷ/noun [C] a bar that connects a pair of wheels on a vehicle 车轴；轮轴

ayatollah
/ˌaɪəˈtɒlə ||; ˌaɪəˈtɑlə/noun [C] a religious leader of Shiite Muslims in Iran 阿亚图拉（伊朗伊斯兰教什叶派领袖）

azalea
/əˈzeɪliə ||; əˈzeljə/noun [C] a plant or bush with large flowers that may be pink, purple, white or yellow 杜鹃花；映山红

azure
/ˈæʒə(r);(brit also 英亦作) ˈæzjʊə(r)||; ˈæʒɚ/adj (written 书面语) bright blue in colour like the sky 天蓝色的；蔚蓝色的 ➔azure noun [U]
